class="mask"><div class="text-slide"><div class="clearfix text-formatted field field--name-field-hotel-description field--type-text-long field--label-hidden field__items"><div class="field__item"><p>The Balearic Islands? The Canary Islands? Greece? No, this year let yourself be tempted by <strong>Martinique</strong>!<br>Go with B&amp;B HOTELS to<strong> </strong>a Caribbean <strong>sun destination</strong> with the <strong>azure</strong> sea of the Caribbean for a direct flight to the Creole landscapes: welcome to our <strong>B&amp;B HOTEL Fort-de-France</strong>!</p><h2>B&amp;B HOTELS in the overseas region: the French West Indies await you!&nbsp;</h2><p>To welcome you for a night or your entire stay on one of the islands of the <strong>Lesser Antilles archipelago</strong>, discover the new B&amp;B HOTELS address: B&amp;B HOTEL Fort-de-France.&nbsp;</p><p>This property offers <strong>71 rooms with a modern design</strong> and tastefully decorated to put you in the atmosphere of the islands as soon as you enter the room. Appropriate this space and be at home, with some rooms having sea views.&nbsp;<br>Located <strong>just a few minutes from the Marinas</strong>, no doubt a boat trip will be in the cards.</p><h2>B&amp;B HOTEL Fort-de-France: a comfortable hotel room overlooking the Bay of Fort-de-France and Les Trois Ilets&nbsp;</h2><p>Located at the tip of the port area of Etang Z'Abricots, our B&amp;B HOTEL Fort-de-France offers a total of 71 rooms including <strong>double rooms</strong> that can accommodate two people and so-called <strong>family</strong> <strong>rooms</strong> with a capacity of up to 4 people. The latter, thanks to their capacity, are ideal for you to stay with family or friends in our establishment.&nbsp;<br>The hotel also has <strong>interconnecting rooms</strong>. If you would like more information or to check their availability during your stay, we invite you to contact our team or stipulate it at the dedicated space when booking on our website.<br>All of our rooms benefit from amenities which have been designed for your comfort and for unparalleled quality: <strong>air conditioning</strong>, queen size bed with mattresses and pillows made in collaboration with French bedding professionals brand. A flat-screen TV is available in each room to provide you with evenings as comfortable as if you were at home. A <strong>private bathroom</strong>, a <strong>work desk,</strong> a luggage holder and opening windows complete the room's furnishings.</p><h2>Book your Paris-Martinique flight and have the B&amp;B HOTEL Fort-de-France reflex!</h2><p><strong>Going to the other end of the world</strong> for a stay in the sun and finding that an economical accommodation solution seems complicated? B&amp;B HOTELS gives you a hand.&nbsp;</p><h2>Why choose our hotel for your stay?&nbsp;</h2><p><strong>Less than 10 minutes from Fort de France </strong>Aimé Césaire Airport, our <strong>sea view hotel</strong> is the ideal residence when you come to the island. A central location that places it in the heart of the city.</p><p>Throughout your city getaway, you'll discover colourful streets where street-art enthusiasts can explore their creativity. From local cuisine restaurants to the many stalls of the markets: be ready to discover new flavours!<br>To relax after a busy day, our B&amp;B HOTEL Fort-de-France offers its <strong>lounge bar&nbsp;("Coming soon")</strong>. The perfect opportunity to share professional or friendly moments that, combined with the menu proposed by our <strong>restaurant</strong>, will help you to perfect your knowledge of culinary art and <strong>Martiniquais* Rums</strong>. Note that we do not offer half board or full board.<br>With an average of 108 hours of sunshine per month and the <strong>pool of our hotel with free access</strong>, evenings by the water with a sea are yours while you are in Fort-de-France!</p><h2>A new destination and always as many B&amp;B HOTELS services&nbsp;</h2><p>Close to the most beautiful beaches of the island, enjoy <strong>access to your room 24/7</strong>. Our team welcomes you at any time, day or night.</p><p>Due to its proximity to the Grand Port Maritime of Martinique, our establishment is an ideal base for you and your teams for a business trip.<br>For this purpose, our B&amp;B HOTEL Fort-de-France offers a seminar room and <strong>an unlimited high-speed WiFi connection</strong>.</p><p>For our guests who drive the island, our hotel has <strong>free private outdoor parking</strong> with 53 spaces. Electric charging stations are also available. If you want to rent a car, don’t hesitate to contact our hotel: we can inform you and accompany you in your search.</p><p>Start the day with a sports session? It is possible in our B&amp;B HOTEL Fort-de-France: with facilities that allow everyone to exercise at their own pace, do not hesitate to go there during your stay in our hotel.</p><p>Our hotel has <strong>rooms adapted to the more specific needs of people with reduced mobility</strong>: more spacious and meeting specific standards, they will allow you to have a peaceful and quiet stay. Bookable from our website, you can leave a message to our team so that we can accompany you throughout your booking.</p><p>At your disposal on request:<br>- baby cots (make sure to request it upon booking, limited availability)<br>- hair dryer<br>- iron<br>- newspapers and daily press</p><p>Travelling in the company of your pet? Pets are accepted in our establishment for an extra charge of €4 per night in our hotel.</p><p><em><span><span><span><span><span>For everyone's comfort, your pet will have to wait patiently in the room while you enjoy the sweet or savoury all-you-can-eat breakfast!</span></span></span></span></span></em><br>&nbsp;</p></div><div class="field__item"><h3>Your breakfast at B&amp;B HOTEL Fort-de-France</h3><p>The<strong> all-you-can eat buffet breakfast</strong> at B&amp;B HOTELS is not to be missed.</p><p>Every morning we pledge to deliver for you "ONLY GOOD FOOD". That’s our promise.</p><p>We work closely with our trusted suppliers to bring you quality produce, with an emphasis on sustainability and "<strong>made in France</strong>" ingredients.</p><p>Whether you prefer something sweet in the morning, a more traditional option, a healthy choice or a hot breakfast, you are sure to find something in our buffet&nbsp; to satisfy your tastes and your appetite!&nbsp;</p><p>Guests love our "tartine" bar, where you can help yourself to fresh breads and spreads, as well as our selection of dairy products and our hot food section.&nbsp;</p><p>And of course no breakfast would be complete without a generous hot drink to start the day (think coffee, tea and hot chocolate), and a refreshing selection of juices.</p><p>Discover the delicious produce that makes up our <a data-entity-substitution="canonical" data-entity-type="node" data-entity-uuid="3f930e6e-1c18-4eb1-8d43-259309e355b3" href="/en/services/france/breakfast">all-you-can-eat breakfast buffet</a> for yourself, as well as the great value for money offered by the price. And for the little ones (up to 10 years inclusive), the full grown-up <strong>breakfast</strong> is on offer for a mini price!</p><h2>Escape to the West Indies and sleep in our 3-star sea view hotel in Fort-de-France&nbsp;</h2><p>Organise your holiday and discover the beautiful <strong>bay</strong> s that punctuate the island and admire the most <strong>beautiful tropical panoramas</strong> while staying at our hotel.</p><p>Thanks to the sea links set up, stop in the <strong>islands of Saint Lucia,</strong> <strong>Guadeloupe</strong> or <strong>Marie-Galante</strong> with regular departures from Fort-de-France (average duration of the crossing: 2 hours depending on the destinations). These international destinations are very popular and never tire the tourists who photograph the beauty of sandy beaches.</p><p>Fan of land trips? Follow the coastal trails, including 10 marked walking tours, explore <strong>Fort Saint-Louis</strong> and let yourself be guided by hummingbirds singing in the <strong>Balata Garden</strong>.<br>In the south of the island, enjoy the <strong>seaside resort of Pointe du Bout aux Trois-Ilets</strong>, Anses d'Arlet or the Diamant Beach that await you for swimming and relaxing: ideal for isolating yourself from the rest of the world for a few hours!</p><p>For your next holidays and stays in Martinique, remember to book your double or family room on our website to benefit from the best rates and promotions in our <strong>B&amp;B HOTEL Fort-de-France. </strong><br>&nbsp;</p><p><em>*Alcohol abuse is dangerous to your health. Consume in moderation.</em></p></div></div></div></div> <a href="#" class="link-more"> <span>Read more</span> <span class="less">View fewer details</span> </a></div></div><div class="reviews-block Do you provide baby beds?</p></div></h2></div><div class="faq-list__answer slide" style="display: none;"><div class="wysiwyg-block"><div class="clearfix text-formatted field field--name-field-answer-faq-hotel field--type-text-long field--label-hidden field__item"><p>This can vary from one hotel to another for reasons of safety.</p><p>So please contact the hotel at which you want to book directly during reception opening hours.&nbsp;<a data-entity-substitution="canonical" data-entity-type="node" data-entity-uuid="0dcc7af2-33d5-42bf-8dc5-f4405bcbe08c" class="faq-list__question"> <span class="faq-list__opener opener"></span><h2><div class="field field--name-field-question-faq-hotel field--type-string-long field--label-hidden field__item"><p>Must I pay for a supplement for my cat or my dog?</p></div></h2></div><div class="faq-list__answer slide" style="display: none;"><div class="wysiwyg-block"><div class="clearfix text-formatted field field--name-field-answer-faq-hotel field--type-text-long field--label-hidden field__item"><p>We gladly welcome your pet.</p><p>It must be kept on its leash and can accompany you in your room for a supplement of €4 per night*.</p><p>Naturally, it will not be allowed into the breakfast room for the well-being of all the guests.</p><p>&nbsp;</p><p>*€9 per night at the B&amp;B Hotel Saint-Jean-de-Luz</p></div></div></div></li><li class="DJ__accordionFaqClickHotel__processed faq-list__item" data-faqid="39251"><div class="faq-list__question"> <span class="faq-list__opener opener"></span><h2><div class="field field--name-field-question-faq-hotel field--type-string-long field--label-hidden field__item"><p>Can I pay for my stay using holiday field--type-text-long field--label-hidden field__item"><p>Of course! You can pay for your stay using holiday vouchers when you arrive at the hotel during reception opening hours.</p><p>Important: you cannot pay using holiday vouchers when booking a promotional offer,
